(Beyer 1992: 83) suggest that བསྐྱར is a palatalized version of བསྐྱརད , however བསྐྱར has the root vowel o and སྐྱོར the root vowel a, so his analysis is unlikely.

འགོད|Present: གོད KYT, KYN, TD, LZ, CD, ND, DK, DS, TC. འཁོད LZ.\nPast: སྐོ KYTC, ཁོད KYTZ,ཁོས KYN, TD, LZ, CD, ND, DK, DS, TC.\nFuture: མཁོས KYT, KYN, TD, LZ, CD, ND, DK, DS, TC. འགོ CD.\nImperative: འཁོད KYT, KYNZ (see note), LZ, ND, CD, DS, TC. རྒྱན་དང་བདེ་དང་བྲལ་སོགས KYNC, TD, LZ, (DS). གྲལ་དང་གནས་སུ DK\nVoluntary: KYT, KYN, TD, CD, ND, DS, TC, (Hoshi 2003).\nTransitive: DS, TC.\nSyntax: [Erg. Abs.] (Hackett 2003).\nCausative of: ཚོམ་བུ་དང་ཡི་གེར་སོགས་སུ (Beyer 1992: 112), (Gyurme 1992: 259), (Duff).གནས་སུ (Chang vii.19, see note)\nCharacteristic Example: འགོ TD, འཁོད ('god) LZ, འགོད (dgod) LZ. འཁོད ND.\nMeaning: 1. To design, project, plan; to found, establish, lay out; to fix, put ('god) CD. To build, arrange, plan (bkod) CD. To register, make a record; to coronate, enthrone; to make peace; to put a signature or seal on DK. 1. To insert, to establish, to put, to secure. to rectify. 2. To design, to formulate, to plan out, to build, to lay out. 3. To write, to sign, to record, to document TC.\nNote: Root given as *go+d (Chang 1971: vii.18).\nNote:KYNZ has an erasure of one character i.e. ཁོད may have been the original reading. (Chang 1971: vii.18) suggests that 'god functions as a causative of འཁོད in Lhasa dialect. (Uray 1972: 19) connects this verb with དགོད /_བཀོད /_འགོད 'institution, administration, settlement of the state' along with the verbs, བགོད and དགོད. (Takeuchi 1990: 175) suggests that the noun འགོད 'order to execute' is derived from the intransitive perfect form of this verb.

However in the body of the dictionary under 'gyur the first definition is listed without verb stems. The second definition is listed with the stems: གྱུརད , འགྱུརད , འགྱུར , - with the definition 'to be established, or arise different than before'. (Li yung khrang 1988) which is supposed to be an excerpt of verb material form TC is exactly the same but lists defintion one with the stems: 'gyur, 'gyur, 'gyur, -. (Hoshi 2003) also distinguishes two verbs NWH.

(Chang 1984) conjectures that the termination -b is original. This verb is frequently added to nouns to form new verbs, it generally indicates a voluntary verb, whereas རྒྱོབ is used in the same way to indicate lack of volition or to show that the action was well done (Chang 1984).

The relationship between these three verbs (བརྒྱགས , རྒྱག , རྒྱགས ) is hardly clear.

རྒྱང|Present: རྐྱོང (CD), DK. \nPast: རྒྱོང DK.\nFuture: རྒྱངས DK.\nImperative: བརྒྱང DK.\nMeaning: To stretch, extend, stretch forth (one's hands to a person), put out (the tongue); spread; distend (the wings, a curtain) CD. To cause to be delayed; to extend DK.\nNote: Root given as rgyang < *gryang (Beyer 1992: 85).\nNote: Compare བརྒྱངས and རྒྱང.
རྒྱན|Present: རྒྱན་དང་དར་སོགས་ཀྱིས LZ, DK, DS, TC. \nPast: རྒྱན LZ, DK རྒྱན DS, TC.\nFuture: རྒྱནད LZ, DK, DS, TC.\nImperative: བརྒྱན LZ, DK. བརྒྱན DS, TC.\nVoluntary: DS, TC.\nTransitive: DS, TC.\nSyntax: [Erg. Abs.] (Hackett 2003).\nDenominative of: བརྒྱནད 'ornament' (Beyer 1992: 111)\nCharacteristic Example: རྒྱན LZ.\nMeaning: To ornament; to beautify or to decorate, to wear or to put on DK. To adorn, ornament DS. To adorn, ornament, to decorate TC.

གསོལ|Present: སྤྲིང LZ. སྩོལ CD, ND, DS, TC. \nPast: མཆིད་གསོལ་པ LZ, ND. ཞལ་དུ [DS], TC.\nFuture: མཆི་དང་བཞལ་དུ LZ, ND, [DS], TC.\nImperative: ཞུ་དོན་སོགས LZ, ND. གསོལ CD. - ND. སོལ TC.\nVoluntary: ND, CD, TC, (Hoshi 2003). (གསོལད ) To send a letter (from a person of lower rank to a person of higher rank) (Takeuchi 1990: 183).\nNote: Compare གསོལ and གསོལད.
